      - should test locked check with different vaults
      - should test isVault check with hub configuration
    Edge cases and permutations
      - should handle all boolean flag permutations
      - should test multiple vault addresses
      - should test all TEST functions in sequence

  VFIDEToken basic flows
    - pre-mints dev reserve to vesting vault
    - allows owner to disable vaultOnly and set presale, presale mints within cap
    - transfers update balances

  VFIDEToken edge cases and fee routing
    - presale cap is enforced
    - fee routing: burn + sanctum to treasury sink
    - policy lock prevents disabling critical modules
    - vaultOnly enforces transfers when enabled

  VFIDEToken additional behaviors
    - approve/increase/decrease allowance and transferFrom
    - systemExempt bypasses vaultOnly and fees
    - securityHub lock prevents transfers involving locked vaults
    - burn sink receives burn amount instead of hard burn
